		id = SOV_tank_tractors
		icon = GFX_tractors_for_tanks
		prerequisite = { focus = SOV_tankograd }
		prerequisite = { focus = SOV_sacrifice }
		x = 1
		y = 3
		relative_position_id = SOV_tankograd
		cost = 35 # Previously was: 35.0 
		available = {

		}
		
		completion_reward = {
			set_temp_variable = { goodies = tractor_plants }
			set_temp_variable = { goodies_tank = goodies }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { goodies_tank > 5 } }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { goodies_tank = 5 }
				divide_temp_variable = { goodies_tank = 2 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { goodies_tank = 5 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { goodies_tank > 15 } }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { goodies_tank = 15 }
				divide_temp_variable = { goodies_tank = 2 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { goodies_tank = 10 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { goodies_tank > 35 } }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { goodies_tank = 35 }
				divide_temp_variable = { goodies_tank = 2 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { goodies_tank = 15 }
			}
			round_temp_variable = goodies_tank
			clamp_temp_variable = {
				var = goodies_tank
				max = 40
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { goodies_tank > 5 } }
				set_variable = { goodies_onmap = goodies_tank }
				subtract_from_variable = { goodies_onmap = 5 }     
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { goodies_tank = goodies_onmap }
			}
			multiply_temp_variable = { goodies_tank = 2 }
			add_offsite_building = { type = tank_assembly level = goodies_tank }
			add_to_variable = { offsite/tank_assembly = goodies_tank }
			
			SOV_create_onmap_tank_assembly = yes
			
			multiply_temp_variable = { goodies = 4 }
			add_offsite_building = { type = arms_factory level = goodies }
			divide_temp_variable = { goodies = 10 }
			round_variable = goodies
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { goodies < 2 }
				}
				add_tech_bonus = {
					name = SOV_tank_tractors
					bonus = 0.15
					uses = 1
					category = armor_tech
					
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { goodies < 4 }
				}
				add_tech_bonus = {
					name = SOV_tank_tractors
					bonus = 0.15
					uses = 2
					category = armor_tech
					
				}	
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { goodies < 6 }
				}
				add_tech_bonus = {
					name = SOV_tank_tractors
					bonus = 0.15
					uses = 3
					category = armor_tech
					
				}	
			}
			else = {
				add_tech_bonus = {
					name = SOV_tank_tractors
					bonus = 0.15
					uses = 5
					category = armor_tech
					
				}	
			}
